main dispatch loop in OpenJDK/JDK is implemented across multiple interconnected C++ files:\\n\\n## Bytecode Dispatch Table (Core Components)\\n\\nThe bytecode dispatch mechanism is centrally defined in:\\n\\n1. **src/hotspot/share/interpreter/templateInterpreter.hpp**: Defines the `DispatchTable` class which contains dispatch tables indexed by tosca (Top-Of-Stack CAche) state and bytecode value. Each entry is a 256-element table (one for each possible bytecode, since `length = 1 << BitsPerByte`). The `EntryPoint` class groups tosca-specific entry points into units. Three dispatch tables are maintained: `_active_table` (currently used by interpreter), `_normal_table` (normal mode), and `_safept_table` (safepoint mode).\\n\\n2. **src/hotspot/share/interpreter/templateInterpreter.cpp**: Contains the actual dispatch table implementations and initialization of all three dispatch tables (`_active_table`, `_normal_table`, `_safept_table`) as well as wide instruction entry points (`_wentry_point`). Also defines return entry points for various invoke bytecodes.\\n\\n## Interpreter Template Generation\\n\\nThe template-based code generation system is implemented in:\\n\\n1. **src/hotspot/share/interpreter/templateInterpreterGenerator.hpp**: Defines the `TemplateInterpreterGenerator` class which generates interpreter templates.\\n\\n2. **src/hotspot/share/interpreter/templateInterpreterGenerator.cpp**: Contains core template generation logic:\\n   - `generate_all()`: Main method that generates all interpreter templates\\n   - `set_entry_points_for_all_bytes()`: Populates dispatch table entries for all bytecodes\\n   - `set_entry_points(Bytecodes::Code code)`: Sets up entry points for a specific bytecode\\n   - `generate_and_dispatch()`: Handles bytecode code generation and dispatch\\n   - Various helper methods for counting bytecodes, tracing, and histogram generation\\n\\n3. **src/hotspot/share/interpreter/templateTable.hpp/cpp**: Defines the `Template` class which describes properties and code generators for each bytecode. Each bytecode has a corresponding template that specifies its behavior and how to generate its code.\\n\\n## Main Interpreter Initialization\\n\\n**src/hotspot/share/interpreter/interpreter.cpp**: Contains the main interpreter initialization functions:\\n- `interpreter_init_stub()`: Calls `Interpreter::initialize_stub()`\\n- `interpreter_init_code()`: Calls `Interpreter::initialize_code()`\\n- `InterpreterCodelet`: Represents a single interpreter code unit\\n- `CodeletMark`: Manages code generation for individual codelets\\n\\n## Architecture-Specific Implementations\\n\\nEach CPU architecture implements the bytecode dispatch mechanism with platform-specific optimizations:\\n\\n### X86/X86-64:\\n- **src/hotspot/cpu/x86/templateInterpreterGenerator_x86.cpp**: Base x86 interpreter generator\\n- **src/hotspot/cpu/x86/templateInterpreterGenerator_x86_32.cpp**: 32-bit x86 specifics\\n- **src/hotspot/cpu/x86/templateInterpreterGenerator_x86_64.cpp**: 64-bit x86-64 specifics\\n- **src/hotspot/cpu/x86/templateTable_x86.cpp/hpp**: X86-specific bytecode templates\\n- **src/hotspot/cpu/x86/interp_masm_x86.cpp**: Assembly macro implementation with `dispatch_base()` and `dispatch_only_normal()` methods that use the dispatch table to route to bytecode handlers\\n- **src/hotspot/cpu/x86/abstractInterpreter_x86.cpp**: Abstract interpreter specifics\\n\\n### main dispatch loop in OpenJDK/JDK is implemented across multiple interconnected C++ files:\\n\\n## Bytecode Dispatch Table (Core Components)\\n\\nThe bytecode dispatch mechanism is centrally defined in:\\n\\n1. **src/hotspot/share/interpreter/templateInterpreter.hpp**: Defines the `DispatchTable` class which contains dispatch tables indexed by tosca (Top-Of-Stack CAche) state and bytecode value. Each entry is a 256-element table (one for each possible bytecode, since `length = 1 << BitsPerByte`). The `EntryPoint` class groups tosca-specific entry points into units. Three dispatch tables are maintained: `_active_table` (currently used by interpreter), `_normal_table` (normal mode), and `_safept_table` (safepoint mode).\\n\\n2. **src/hotspot/share/interpreter/templateInterpreter.cpp**: Contains the actual dispatch table implementations and initialization of all three dispatch tables (`_active_table`, `_normal_table`, `_safept_table`) as well as wide instruction entry points (`_wentry_point`). Also defines return entry points for various invoke bytecodes.\\n\\n## Interpreter Template Generation\\n\\nThe template-based code generation system is implemented in:\\n\\n1. **src/hotspot/share/interpreter/templateInterpreterGenerator.hpp**: Defines the `TemplateInterpreterGenerator` class which generates interpreter templates.\\n\\n2. **src/hotspot/share/interpreter/templateInterpreterGenerator.cpp**: Contains core template generation logic:\\n   - `generate_all()`: Main method that generates all interpreter templates\\n   - `set_entry_points_for_all_bytes()`: Populates dispatch table entries for all bytecodes\\n   - `set_entry_points(Bytecodes::Code code)`: Sets up entry points for a specific bytecode\\n   - `generate_and_dispatch()`: Handles bytecode code generation and dispatch\\n   - Various helper methods for counting bytecodes, tracing, and histogram generation\\n\\n3. **src/hotspot/share/interpreter/templateTable.hpp/cpp**: Defines the `Template` class which describes properties and code generators for each bytecode. Each bytecode has a corresponding template that specifies its behavior and how to generate its code.\\n\\n## Main Interpreter Initialization\\n\\n**src/hotspot/share/interpreter/interpreter.cpp**:
